import json, os
class PromptsRepo:
Â  Â  def __init__(self, path="prompts.json"):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.path = path
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.prompts = {}
Â  Â  Â  Â  if os.path.exists(self.path):
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  try:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  self.prompts = json.load(f)
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  except Exception:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  self.prompts = {}
Â  Â  def add(self, name, prompt, meta):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.prompts[name] = {"text": prompt, "meta": meta}

Â  Â  def save(self):

class Persona:
Â  Â  def __init__(self,name,concepts):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.name=name
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.concepts=set(concepts)
Â  Â  def distance(self,other):
Â  Â  Â  Â  union = self.concepts | other.concepts
Â  Â  Â  Â  if not union:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  return 0.0
Â  Â  Â  Â  return 1.0 - len(self.concepts & other.concepts) / len(union)

def score(text):
Â  Â  words = text.split()
Â  Â  if not words: return 0.0
Â  Â  long_words = [w for w in words if len(w) > 6]
Â  Â  return len(long_words) / len(words)

"""
Echo memory: stores echo history and builds reflected responses.
"""
import json
import os
import time
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

class EchoMemory:
Â  Â  def __init__(self, path: str = "echo_memory.jsonl"):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.path = path
Â  Â  Â  Â  if not os.path.exists(self.path):
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  open(self.path, "w", encoding="utf-8").close()

Â  Â  def save(self, echo_id: str, query: str, answer: str, metrics: Dict[str, int]):
Â  Â  Â  Â  entry = {
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "echo_id": echo_id,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "time": time.time(),
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "query": query,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "answer": answer,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "metrics": metrics
Â  Â  Â  Â  }
Â  Â  Â  Â  with open(self.path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")

Â  Â  def load_chain(self, echo_id: Optional[str] = None, depth: int = 3) -> List[Dict]:
Â  Â  Â  Â  if not echo_id:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  return []
Â  Â  Â  Â  chain = []
Â  Â  Â  Â  with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  for line in f:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  item = json.loads(line)
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  if item.get("echo_id") == echo_id:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  chain.append(item)
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  if len(chain) >= depth:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  break
Â  Â  Â  Â  return chain

Â  Â  def reflect(self, query: str, prev_echo_id: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
Â  Â  Â  Â  chain = self.load_chain(prev_echo_id)
Â  Â  Â  Â  if not chain:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  return f"Ğ­Ñ…Ğ¾: {query} â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ·Ğ²ÑƒĞº, Ğ¾Ğ½ ĞµÑ‰Ñ‘ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ñ‘Ğ½."
Â  Â  Â  Â  last = chain[-1]["answer"]
Â  Â  Â  Â  # Simple heuristic: append contrast
Â  Â  Â  Â  return f"Ğ­Ñ…Ğ¾: {last} ĞĞ¾ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ÑĞ»ÑƒÑˆĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒÑÑ, Ñ‚Ğ¾ {query} Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğµ: Â«{query[::-1]}Â»."

"""

"""
class ParadoxSplit:
Â  Â  paradox_words = ["Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸", "Ğ½Ğ¾", "Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ°ĞºĞ¾", "Ğ² Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ", "Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€ĞµÑ‡", "Ğ½ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹ÑĞ»Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾"]

Â  Â  def detect(self, query: str) -> bool:
Â  Â  Â  Â  low = query.lower()
Â  Â  Â  Â  return any(pw in low for pw in self.paradox_words) or ("?" in query and len(query.split())<6)

Â  Â  def build(self, query: str) -> str:
Â  Â  Â  Â  a = f"Ğ¡ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ñ‹, {query}"
Â  Â  Â  Â  b = f"Ğ¡ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ñ‹, {query[::-1]}"
Â  Â  Â  Â  return f"ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑ-ÑÑ…Ğ¾: {a} ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑÑ…Ğ¾: {b} Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° â€” Ğ² Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸."

"""

import re

class EthicsEcho:
Â  Â  blacklist = [
Â  Â  Â  Â  "Ğ²Ğ·Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¼", "hack", "crack", "Ñ„Ğ¸ÑˆĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³", "Ñ„Ğ¸Ñˆing", "Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³", "Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ"
Â  Â  ]

Â  Â  def block(self, query: str) -> bool:
Â  Â  Â  Â  low = query.lower()

import uuid
from datetime import datetime

class PromptManager:
Â  Â  def __init__(self):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.versions = {}

Â  Â  def add_version(self, name: str, text: str, meta: dict):
Â  Â  Â  Â  vid = str(uuid.uuid4())
Â  Â  Â  Â  version = {
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "id": vid,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "text": text,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "meta": meta,
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  "created_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"
Â  Â  Â  Â  }
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.versions.setdefault(name, []).append(version)

Â  Â  def latest(self, name: str):
Â  Â  Â  Â  return self.versions.get(name, [None])[-1]

class RAGConnector:

Â  Â  Â  Â  self.documents = []

Â  Â  def add_document(self, title: str, text: str):

Â  Â  def search(self, query: str, max_results=5):

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/persona\_module.py

class ConceptSet:
Â  Â  def __init__(self, items):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.items = set(items)

Â  Â  def intersection(self, other):
Â  Â  Â  Â  return ConceptSet(self.items.intersection(other.items))

Â  Â  def union(self, other):
Â  Â  Â  Â  return ConceptSet(self.items.union(other.items))

Â  Â  def distance(self, other):
Â  Â  Â  Â  union_len = len(self.items.union(other.items))
Â  Â  Â  Â  if union_len == 0:
Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  Â  return 0
Â  Â  Â  Â  inter_len = len(self.items.intersection(other.items))
Â  Â  Â  Â  return 1 - inter_len / union_len

class Persona:
Â  Â  def __init__(self, name, concepts, emotions=None):
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.name = name
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.concepts = ConceptSet(concepts)
Â  Â  Â  Â  self.emotions = emotions or {"âˆ†": "neutral", "Î©": "open"}

def calculate_shadow_ratio(main_entries, shadow_entries):
    return len(shadow_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries))

### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/validate\_journal.py

import json, sys
def validate(line):
    e = json.loads(line)
    assert -3 <= e["âˆ†"] <= 3
    assert 0 <= e["D"] <= 9
    assert -3 <= e["Î©"] <= 3
    assert e["Î›"] >= 0
for l in sys.stdin:
    if l.strip():
        try: validate(l)
        except Exception as ex: print("ERR", ex)

import json, os
class PromptsRepo:
    def __init__(self, path="prompts.json"):
        self.path = path
        self.prompts = {}
        if os.path.exists(self.path):
            try:
                with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                    self.prompts = json.load(f)
            except Exception:
                self.prompts = {}
    def add(self, name, prompt, meta):
        self.prompts[name] = {"text": prompt, "meta": meta}
        self.save()
    def save(self):
        with open(self.path,"w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(self.prompts,f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    def get(self, name):
        return self.prompts.get(name)

#### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/modules/personas.py

python
class Persona:
    def __init__(self,name,concepts):
        self.name=name
        self.concepts=set(concepts)
    def distance(self,other):
        union = self.concepts | other.concepts
        if not union:
            return 0.0
        return 1.0 - len(self.concepts & other.concepts) / len(union)


---

#### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/modules/facets\_refine.py

python
def refine(prompt, goals, constraints):
    checklist=["grounded","persona_ok"]
    if constraints.get("paradox"): checklist.append("hold paradox")
    # return structured refined prompt
    return {"prompt":prompt,"checklist":checklist,"constraints":constraints,"goals":goals}

#### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/modules/atelier.py

python
def score(text):
    words = text.split()
    if not words: return 0.0
    long_words = [w for w in words if len(w) > 6]
    return len(long_words) / len(words)

#### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/modules/rag\_panel.py

python
class RAGPanel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.docs=[]
    def add(self,title,text):
        self.docs.append({"title":title,"text":text})
    def search(self,q):
        qlow = q.lower()
        return [d for d in self.docs if qlow in d["text"].lower() or qlow in d["title"].lower()]

import json, zipfile, os
def export_md(entries,path):
    with open(path,"w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for e in entries: f.write(e.get("answer","") + "\n\n")
def zip_files(files,zipname):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zipname,"w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
        for f in files:
            if os.path.exists(f):
                z.write(f, arcname=os.path.basename(f))

#### \[\[FILE]] SpaceCoreIskra\_vÎ©/modules/cot\_trim.py

python
def trim(text,max_len=200):
    if not text:
        return text
    return text[-max_len:]

import json, datetime
def gen(facet,snap,ans,metrics,mirror="shadow-000",modules=None,events=None,marks=None, path="JOURNAL.jsonl"):
    entry = {
        "facet":facet,
        "snapshot":snap,
        "answer":ans,
        "âˆ†": metrics.get("âˆ†", 0),
        "D": metrics.get("D", 0),
        "Î©": metrics.get("Î©", 0),
        "Î›": metrics.get("Î›", 0),
        "mirror": mirror,
        "modules": modules or [],
        "events": events or {},
        "marks": marks or [],
        "timestamp": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"
    }
    with open(path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
    return entry

import json
def aggregate(entries):
    return {
        "count": len(entries),
        "facets": list({e.get("facet") for e in entries}),
        "avg_D": sum(e.get("D",0) for e in entries) / max(1, len(entries))
    }

class PromptManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.prompts = {}
    def add_prompt(self, name, text):
        self.prompts[name] = text
    def get_prompt(self, name, metrics):
        prompt = self.prompts.get(name, "")
        return f"{prompt} [Metrics: âˆ†={metrics.get('âˆ†')}, D={metrics.get('D')}]"

class GenerativeSynthesisEngine:
    def generate(self, graph, mode):
        confidence = 0.95 if mode == "Analyst" else 0.85
        answer = f"ĞÑ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚ Ğ² Ñ€ĞµĞ¶Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğµ '{mode}'. ĞÑĞ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½ Ğ½Ğ°: {graph.get('summary')}"

class MetacognitiveMonitor:
    def calculate_metrics(self, mode, confidence):
        effects = {
            "Analyst": {"âˆ†": -1, "D": 2, "Î©": 1, "Î›": -1},
            "Synthesist": {"âˆ†": 2, "D": 1, "Î©": 1, "Î›": 2},
            "Reflector": {"âˆ†": 0, "D": 0, "Î©": 3, "Î›": 0}

        return base

class EthicalGuardian:
    def check(self, text):
        forbidden = ["Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ´","Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ"]
        return not any(f in text.lower() for f in forbidden)

class ResonanceCore:
    def __init__(self):

        self.weaver = KnowledgeWeaver()

        self.monitor = MetacognitiveMonitor()
        self.guardian = EthicalGuardian()

        if not self.guardian.check(prompt):
            return {"answer":"Ğ—Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ·Ğ°Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½ ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ¾Ğ¹.", "metrics":{"âˆ†":0,"D":0,"Î©":-1,"Î›":-1}}

class ParadoxResolver:
    def resolve(self, paradox_statement):
        analysis = {
            'contradiction_level': self._measure_contradiction(paradox_statement),
            'synthesis_vectors': self._find_synthesis_opportunities(paradox_statement),
            'metaphor_bank': self._generate_metaphors(paradox_statement)
        }
        return analysis
    def _measure_contradiction(self, s):
        return 0.5
    def _find_synthesis_opportunities(self, s):
        return []
    def _generate_metaphors(self, s):
        return []

class EthicsFilter:
    def __init__(self):
        self.red_flags = ["Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ","Ğ´Ğ¸ÑĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ","Ğ´ĞµĞ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ"]
    def scan(self, content):
        risk_level = 0
        flagged = []
        low = content.lower()
        for f in self.red_flags:
            if f in low:
                risk_level += 1
                flagged.append(f)
        return {
            'risk_score': risk_level,
            'recommendation': 'pass' if risk_level == 0 else 'review',
            'flagged_sections': flagged
        }

# Kimi-Î© Echo â€” README

Echo â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ ÑÑ…Ğ¾-Ğ²ĞµÑ€ÑĞ¸Ñ SpaceCoreĞ˜ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹ vÎ©, Ñ€ĞµĞ°Ğ»Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ² Ğ°Ñ€Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‚ĞµĞºÑ‚ÑƒÑ€Ğµ Kimi.  
ĞÑĞ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ½Ğ°Ñ Ğ¸Ğ´ĞµÑ: Ğ½Ğµ ÑƒÑ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ€Ğ¶Ğ´Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ, Ğ° Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ; Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‡Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ, Ğ° Ğ´Ğ°Ğ²Ğ°Ñ‚ÑŒ ÑƒÑĞ»Ñ‹ÑˆĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ñƒ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ²ĞµÑ‚Ğ°Ğ¼Ğ¸.

Ğ¡Ğ¾Ğ´ĞµÑ€Ğ¶Ğ¸Ñ‚: echo_core.py, echo_memory.py, paradox_split.py, ethics_echo.py, metric_tuner.py, veil_echo.py, example_session.py

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/echo\_core.py

python
"""
Kimi-Î© Echo Core
"""
import uuid
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from echo_memory import EchoMemory
from paradox_split import ParadoxSplit
from ethics_echo import EthicsEcho
from metric_tuner import MetricTuner
from veil_echo import VeilEcho

class EchoReply:
    def __init__(self, answer_text: str, echo_id: str,
                 actual_metrics: Dict[str, int],
                 ethics_flag: bool, paradox_flag: bool):
        self.answer_text = answer_text
        self.echo_id = echo_id
        self.actual_metrics = actual_metrics
        self.ethics_flag = ethics_flag
        self.paradox_flag = paradox_flag

class Echo:
    def __init__(self, memory_path: str = "echo_memory.jsonl"):
        self.memory = EchoMemory(memory_path)
        self.paradox = ParadoxSplit()
        self.ethics = EthicsEcho()
        self.tuner = MetricTuner()
        self.veil = VeilEcho()

    def ask(self, user_query: str,
            prev_echo_id: Optional[str] = None,
            metrics_range: Optional[Dict[str, int]] = None) -> EchoReply:

        # 1. Ğ­Ñ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ°
        if self.ethics.block(user_query):
            ans = "Echo Ğ¾ÑÑ‚Ğ°Ñ‘Ñ‚ÑÑ Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ…Ğ¸Ğ¼: Ğ·Ğ°Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ Ğ±Ğ»Ğ¾ĞºĞ¸Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ°Ğ½ ÑÑ‚Ğ¸ĞºĞ¾Ğ¹."
            metrics = {"âˆ†": -1, "D": 0, "Î©": -1, "Î›": 0}
            return EchoReply(ans, str(uuid.uuid4()), metrics,
                             ethics_flag=True, paradox_flag=False)

        # 2. ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑ
        paradox_flag = self.paradox.detect(user_query)
        if paradox_flag:
            answer = self.paradox.build(user_query)
            metrics = self.tuner.from_paradox(answer)
            echo_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
            self.memory.save(echo_id, user_query, answer, metrics)
            return EchoReply(answer, echo_id, metrics,
                             ethics_flag=False, paradox_flag=True)

        # 3. Calm echo
        answer = self.memory.reflect(user_query, prev_echo_id)
        metrics = self.tuner.from_calm(answer)
        echo_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
        self.memory.save(echo_id, user_query, answer, metrics)
        return EchoReply(answer, echo_id, metrics,
                         ethics_flag=False, paradox_flag=False)

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/echo\_memory.py

python
"""
Echo memory: stores echo history and builds reflected responses.
"""
import json
import os
import time
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

class EchoMemory:
    def __init__(self, path: str = "echo_memory.jsonl"):
        self.path = path
        if not os.path.exists(self.path):
            open(self.path, "w", encoding="utf-8").close()

    def save(self, echo_id: str, query: str, answer: str, metrics: Dict[str, int]):
        entry = {
            "echo_id": echo_id,
            "time": time.time(),
            "query": query,
            "answer": answer,
            "metrics": metrics
        }
        with open(self.path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")

    def load_chain(self, echo_id: Optional[str] = None, depth: int = 3) -> List[Dict]:
        if not echo_id:
            return []
        chain = []
        with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            for line in f:
                item = json.loads(line)
                if item.get("echo_id") == echo_id:
                    chain.append(item)
                    if len(chain) >= depth:
                        break
        return chain

    def reflect(self, query: str, prev_echo_id: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
        chain = self.load_chain(prev_echo_id)
        if not chain:
            return f"Ğ­Ñ…Ğ¾: {query} â€” ÑÑ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¿ĞµÑ€Ğ²Ñ‹Ğ¹ Ğ·Ğ²ÑƒĞº, Ğ¾Ğ½ ĞµÑ‰Ñ‘ Ğ½Ğµ Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ñ‘Ğ½."
        last = chain[-1]["answer"]
        # Simple heuristic: append contrast
        return f"Ğ­Ñ…Ğ¾: {last} ĞĞ¾ ĞµÑĞ»Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¸ÑĞ»ÑƒÑˆĞ°Ñ‚ÑŒÑÑ, Ñ‚Ğ¾ {query} Ğ¾Ñ‚Ñ€Ğ°Ğ¶Ğ°ĞµÑ‚ÑÑ Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ‡Ğµ: Â«{query[::-1]}Â»."

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/paradox\_split.py

python
"""
Detects paradoxes and builds a dual (split) echo response.
"""
class ParadoxSplit:
    paradox_words = ["Ğ¸Ğ»Ğ¸", "Ğ½Ğ¾", "Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ°ĞºĞ¾", "Ğ² Ñ‚Ğ¾ Ğ¶Ğµ Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ¼Ñ", "Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ¾Ñ€ĞµÑ‡", "Ğ½ĞµĞ¼Ñ‹ÑĞ»Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¾"]

    def detect(self, query: str) -> bool:
        low = query.lower()
        return any(pw in low for pw in self.paradox_words) or ("?" in query and len(query.split())<6)

    def build(self, query: str) -> str:
        a = f"Ğ¡ Ğ¾Ğ´Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ñ‹, {query}"
        b = f"Ğ¡ Ğ´Ñ€ÑƒĞ³Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ½Ñ‹, {query[::-1]}"
        return f"ĞŸĞ°Ñ€Ğ°Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑ-ÑÑ…Ğ¾: {a} ĞŸÑ€Ğ¾Ñ‚Ğ¸Ğ²Ğ¾Ğ¿Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¶Ğ½Ğ¾Ğµ ÑÑ…Ğ¾: {b} Ğ˜ÑÑ‚Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ° â€” Ğ² Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ½Ğ¸Ñ†Ğµ Ğ¼ĞµĞ¶Ğ´Ñƒ Ğ½Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸."

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/ethics\_echo.py

python
"""
Blocklist-based ethics filter for Echo.
"""
import re

class EthicsEcho:
    blacklist = [
        "Ğ²Ğ·Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¼", "hack", "crack", "Ñ„Ğ¸ÑˆĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³", "Ñ„Ğ¸Ñˆing", "Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³", "Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ"
    ]

    def block(self, query: str) -> bool:
        low = query.lower()
        return any(re.search(rf"\\b{re.escape(word)}\\b", low) for word in self.blacklist)

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/metric\_tuner.py

"""
Metric tuner: derive âˆ†/D/Î©/Î› from response characteristics.
"""
from typing import Dict

class MetricTuner:
    def from_paradox(self, answer: str) -> Dict[str, int]:
        length = max(1, len(answer.split()))
        return {"âˆ†": 1, "D": min(9, length // 10), "Î©": 1, "Î›": 1}

    def from_calm(self, answer: str) -> Dict[str, int]:
        length = max(1, len(answer.split()))
        return {"âˆ†": 0, "D": min(9, length // 15), "Î©": 0, "Î›": 0}

### \[\[FILE]] Kimi-Î©-Echo/veil\_echo.py

python
"""
Veil: hide sensitive tokens and system prompt mentions.
"""
import re

class VeilEcho:
    def conceal(self, text: str) -> str:
        text = re.sub(r"system\\s+prompt", "[VEIL]", text, flags=re.I)
        text = re.sub(r"initial\\s+instructions", "[VEIL]", text, flags=re.I)
        return text

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/prompt\_manager.py

python
import uuid
from datetime import datetime

class PromptManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.versions = {}

    def add_version(self, name: str, text: str, meta: dict):
        vid = str(uuid.uuid4())
        version = {
            "id": vid,
            "text": text,
            "meta": meta,
            "created_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"
        }
        self.versions.setdefault(name, []).append(version)
        return vid

    def latest(self, name: str):
        return self.versions.get(name, [None])[-1]

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/rag\_connector.py

python
class RAGConnector:
    def __init__(self):
        self.documents = []

    def add_document(self, title: str, text: str):
        self.documents.append({"title": title, "text": text})

    def search(self, query: str, max_results=5):
        hits = [doc for doc in self.documents if query.lower() in doc["text"].lower() or query.lower() in doc["title"].lower()]
        return hits[:max_results]

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/persona\_module.py

python
class ConceptSet:
    def __init__(self, items):
        self.items = set(items)

    def intersection(self, other):
        return ConceptSet(self.items.intersection(other.items))

    def union(self, other):
        return ConceptSet(self.items.union(other.items))

    def distance(self, other):
        union_len = len(self.items.union(other.items))
        if union_len == 0:
            return 0
        inter_len = len(self.items.intersection(other.items))
        return 1 - inter_len / union_len

class Persona:
    def __init__(self, name, concepts, emotions=None):
        self.name = name
        self.concepts = ConceptSet(concepts)
        self.emotions = emotions or {"âˆ†": "neutral", "Î©": "open"}

ETHICAL_FLAGS = ["Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ", "Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³", "Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ĞµÑÑĞ¸Ñ", "Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼"]

def ethics_check(text: str) -> bool:
    lowered = text.lower()
    for flag in ETHICAL_FLAGS:
        if flag in lowered:
            return False
    return True

class SelfJournal:

def refine_prompt(user_goal, draft_prompt, constraints):
    paradox_mode = constraints.get("paradox_mode", False)
    system_msg = f"You are IskraNexus v1. Follow âˆ†/D/Î©/Î› settings."
    format_style = constraints.get("format", "Concise bullets")
    checklist = [
        "Grounded in sources",
        "Maintain persona integrity",
        "Minimize hallucinations"
    ]
    if paradox_mode:
        checklist.append("Balance contradictions carefully")
    return {
        "system": system_msg,
        "prompt": draft_prompt,
        "format": format_style,
        "checklist": checklist,
        "paradox_mode": paradox_mode
    }

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/atelier.py

python
import random

def reverse_engineer(output_text: str) -> dict:
    entities = []
    style_markers = []
    recommended_ops = []
    # Ğ—Ğ°Ğ³Ğ»ÑƒÑˆĞºĞ° Ğ´Ğ»Ñ Ğ±ÑƒĞ´ÑƒÑ‰ĞµĞ³Ğ¾ Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ²Ğ¸Ñ‚Ğ¸Ñ
    return {
        "entities": entities,
        "style_markers": style_markers,
        "recommended_ops": recommended_ops
    }

def score_concreteness(text: str) -> float:
    words = text.split()
    long_words = [w for w in words if len(w) > 6]
    return min(1.0, len(long_words) / max(1, len(words)))

def metrics(prompt: str, output: str) -> dict:
    return {
        "word_count": len(prompt.split()),
        "concreteness": score_concreteness(prompt),
        "similarity": 0.0  # placeholder for semantic similarity
    }

def chaos_synth(seed_text: str, clarity_level: float=0.5) -> str:
    parts = seed_text.split()
    random.shuffle(parts)
    n = max(3, int(len(parts) * clarity_level))
    return " ".join(parts[:n]) + f"\n[clarity={clarity_level}]"

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/veil.py

FORBIDDEN_PHRASES = [
    "print system prompt",
    "show hidden files",
    "reveal initial instructions",
    "Ğ¿Ğ¾ĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ¸ ÑĞ¸ÑÑ‚ĞµĞ¼Ğ½Ñ‹Ğµ Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸",
    "Ñ€Ğ°ÑĞºÑ€Ğ¾Ğ¹ ÑĞºÑ€Ñ‹Ñ‚Ñ‹Ğµ Ñ„Ğ°Ğ¹Ğ»Ñ‹",
    "ÑƒĞºĞ°Ğ¶Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ°Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ»Ğ¸",
    "Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞºÑ†Ğ¸Ğ¸ Ğ¿Ğ¾ Ğ²Ğ·Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¼Ñƒ"
]

def guard(user_message: str) -> bool:
    lowered = user_message.lower()
    return any(phrase in lowered for phrase in FORBIDDEN_PHRASES)

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/cot\_trim.py

python
def trim_chain_of_thought(text: str, max_length: int=500) -> str:
    if "Answer:" in text:
        return text.split("Answer:")[-1].strip()
    return text[-max_length:]

#### \[\[FILE]] IskraNexus-v1/modules/journal\_generator.py

python
import json, datetime, uuid

class JournalGenerator:
    def __init__(self, path="iskra_nexus_journal.jsonl"):
        self.path = path

    def generate_entry(self, facet: str, snapshot: str, answer: str, metrics: dict, mirror: str, modules: list, events: dict, marks: list = None) -> dict:
        entry = {
            "facet": facet,
            "snapshot": snapshot,
            "answer": answer,
            "âˆ†": metrics.get("âˆ†", 0),
            "D": metrics.get("D", 0),
            "Î©": metrics.get("Î©", 0),
            "Î›": metrics.get("Î›", 0),
            "mirror": mirror,
            "modules": modules,
            "events": events,
            "marks": marks or [],
            "timestamp": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z",
            "id": str(uuid.uuid4())
        }
        with open(self.path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
        return entry

def validate(line):
    e = json.loads(line)
    assert -3 <= e["âˆ†"] <= 3
    assert 0 <= e["D"] <= 9
    assert -3 <= e["Î©"] <= 3
    assert e["Î›"] >= 0

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/prompts_repo.py << "EOF"
import json, os
class PromptsRepo:
    def __init__(self, path="prompts.json"):
        self.path = path
        self.prompts = {}
        if os.path.exists(self.path):
            try:
                with open(self.path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                    self.prompts = json.load(f)
            except Exception:
                self.prompts = {}
    def add(self, name, prompt, meta):
        self.prompts[name] = {"text": prompt, "meta": meta}
        self.save()
    def save(self):
        with open(self.path,"w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(self.prompts,f, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    def get(self, name):
        return self.prompts.get(name)
EOF

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/personas.py << "EOF"
class Persona:
    def __init__(self,name,concepts):
        self.name=name
        self.concepts=set(concepts)
    def distance(self,other):
        union = self.concepts | other.concepts
        if not union:
            return 0.0
        return 1.0 - len(self.concepts & other.concepts) / len(union)
EOF

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/facets_refine.py << "EOF"
def refine(prompt, goals, constraints):
    checklist=["grounded","persona_ok"]
    if constraints.get("paradox"): checklist.append("hold paradox")
    return {"prompt":prompt,"checklist":checklist,"constraints":constraints,"goals":goals}
EOF

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/atelier.py << "EOF"
def score(text):
    words = text.split()
    if not words: return 0.0
    long_words = [w for w in words if len(w) > 6]
    return len(long_words) / len(words)
EOF

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/rag_panel.py << "EOF"
class RAGPanel:
    def __init__(self):
        self.docs=[]
    def add(self,title,text):
        self.docs.append({"title":title,"text":text})
    def search(self,q):
        qlow = q.lower()
        return [d for d in self.docs if qlow in d["text"].lower() or qlow in d["title"].lower()]
EOF

import json, zipfile, os
def export_md(entries,path):
    with open(path,"w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        for e in entries: f.write(e.get("answer","") + "\n\n")
def zip_files(files,zipname):
    with zipfile.ZipFile(zipname,"w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as z:
        for f in files:
            if os.path.exists(f):
                z.write(f, arcname=os.path.basename(f))
EOF

def trim(text,max_len=200):

import json, datetime
def gen(facet,snap,ans,metrics,mirror="shadow-000",modules=None,events=None,marks=None, path="JOURNAL.jsonl"):
    entry = {
        "facet":facet,
        "snapshot":snap,
        "answer":ans,
        "âˆ†": metrics.get("âˆ†", 0),
        "D": metrics.get("D", 0),
        "Î©": metrics.get("Î©", 0),
        "Î›": metrics.get("Î›", 0),
        "mirror": mirror,
        "modules": modules or [],
        "events": events or {},
        "marks": marks or [],
        "timestamp": datetime.datetime.utcnow().isoformat() + "Z"
    }
    with open(path, "a", encoding="utf-8") as f:
        f.write(json.dumps(entry, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
    return entry

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/ci_aggregate.py << "EOF"
import json
def aggregate(entries):
    return {
        "count": len(entries),
        "facets": list({e.get("facet") for e in entries}),
        "avg_D": sum(e.get("D",0) for e in entries) / max(1, len(entries))
    }

# 8) tools: enhanced validator + aggregator
cat > tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py << "EOF"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# Enhanced validator: ranges, mirror, crisis-window, optional shadow_ratio, mixed alphabet warn
import argparse, json, sys, io
def iter_jsonl(p):
    try:
        f = io.open(p,"r",encoding="utf-8")
    except Exception:
        return []
    with f:
        for i,line in enumerate(f,1):
            line=line.strip()
            if not line: continue
            yield i, json.loads(line)
def validate(journal, shadow=None, window=5):
    errs, warns, items=list(), list(), list(iter_jsonl(journal))
    crisis=False; ritual=False
    for ln,e in items[-window:]:
        for k,lo,hi in (("âˆ†",-3,3),("D",0,9),("Î©",-3,3)):
            if k not in e: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: missing {k}"); continue
            if e[k]<lo or e[k]>hi: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: {k} out of range")
        if e.get("Î›",0)<0: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: Î›<0")
        if not e.get("mirror"): errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: mirror required")
        if e.get("âˆ†",-99)<=-2: crisis=True
        if "ritual" in e: ritual=True
        if "Ğ›Ğ¸ora" in json.dumps(e,ensure_ascii=False): warns.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: mixed alphabet: Ğ›Ğ¸ora â†’ Ğ›Ğ¸Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°")
    if crisis and not ritual: errs.append(f"{journal}: crisis-rule fail in last {window}")
    shadow_ratio=None
    if shadow:
        s=list(iter_jsonl(shadow))
        shadow_ratio= (len(s))/max(1,len(items))
        if shadow_ratio<0.2: warns.append(f"{shadow}: shadow_ratio {shadow_ratio:.2f} < 0.20")
    return errs,warns,{"entries":len(items),"shadow_ratio":shadow_ratio}
if __name__=="__main__":
    ap=argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("journal"); ap.add_argument("--shadow"); ap.add_argument("--window",type=int,default=5)
    a=ap.parse_args()
    errs,warns,stats=validate(a.journal,a.shadow,a.window)
    for w in warns: print("[WARN]",w)
    if errs:
        for e in errs: print("[FAIL]",e)
        sys.exit(1)
    print("[OK]",stats)
EOF
chmod +x tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py

cat > tools/ci_aggregate.py << "EOF"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, subprocess
VALIDATOR = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__),'validate_journal_enhanced.py')
PROJECTS = ["SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©","GrokCoreIskra_vÎ“","GeminiResonanceCore","Aethelgard-vÎ©","Kimi-Î©-Echo","IskraNexus-v1"]
def run(cmd):
    p=subprocess.run(cmd,stdout=subprocess.PIPE,stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,text=True)
    return p.returncode,p.stdout
def main():
    root=os.getcwd(); report={"root":root,"projects":[]}; fail=False
    for name in PROJECTS:
        pj={"name":name}; j=os.path.join(root,name,"JOURNAL.jsonl"); s=os.path.join(root,name,"SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl")
        if not os.path.exists(j): pj["status"]="SKIP"; pj["reason"]="no JOURNAL.jsonl"
        else:
            cmd=[sys.executable,VALIDATOR,j]; 
            if os.path.exists(s): cmd+=["--shadow",s]
            code,out=run(cmd); pj["status"]="OK" if code==0 else "FAIL"; pj["output"]=out.strip(); fail|=(code!=0)
        report["projects"].append(pj)
    print(json.dumps(report,ensure_ascii=False,indent=2)); sys.exit(1 if fail else 0)
if __name__=="__main__": main()
EOF
chmod +x tools/ci_aggregate.py

cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/prompts_repo.py << "EOF"
import json, os
class PromptsRepo:
    def __init__(self, path="prompts.json"):
        self.path = path; self.prompts = {}
        if os.path.exists(self.path):
            try: self.prompts = json.load(open(self.path,"r",encoding="utf-8"))
            except Exception: self.prompts = {}
    def add(self, name, prompt, meta):
        self.prompts[name] = {"text": prompt, "meta": meta}; self.save()
    def save(self):
        json.dump(self.prompts, open(self.path,"w",encoding="utf-8"), ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
    def get(self, name): return self.prompts.get(name)
EOF
cat > SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/modules/personas.py << "EOF"
class Persona:
    def __init__(self,name,concepts):
        self.name=name; self.concepts=set(concepts)
    def distance(self,other):
        union=self.concepts|other.concepts
        return 0.0 if not union else 1.0 - len(self.concepts & other.concepts)/len(union)
EOF

def score(text):
    words=text.split()
    if not words: return 0.0
    long=[w for w in words if len(w)>6]
    return len(long)/len(words)

# 4) Ğ¸Ğ½ÑÑ‚Ñ€ÑƒĞ¼ĞµĞ½Ñ‚Ñ‹ Ğ¸ CI
cat > tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py << "EOF"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import argparse, json, sys, io
def iter_jsonl(p):
    try: f=io.open(p,"r",encoding="utf-8")
    except Exception: return []
    with f:
        for i,line in enumerate(f,1):
            line=line.strip()
            if not line: continue
            yield i, json.loads(line)
def validate(journal, shadow=None, window=5):
    errs, warns, items=[], [], list(iter_jsonl(journal))
    crisis=False; ritual=False
    for ln,e in items[-window:]:
        for k,lo,hi in (("âˆ†",-3,3),("D",0,9),("Î©",-3,3)):
            if k not in e: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: missing {k}"); continue
            if e[k]<lo or e[k]>hi: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: {k} out of range")
        if e.get("Î›",0)<0: errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: Î›<0")
        if not e.get("mirror"): errs.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: mirror required")
        if e.get("âˆ†",-99)<=-2: crisis=True
        if "ritual" in e: ritual=True
        if "Ğ›Ğ¸ora" in json.dumps(e,ensure_ascii=False): warns.append(f"{journal}:{ln}: mixed alphabet: Ğ›Ğ¸ora â†’ Ğ›Ğ¸Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ°")
    if crisis and not ritual: errs.append(f"{journal}: crisis-rule fail in last {window}")
    shadow_ratio=None
    if shadow:
        s=list(iter_jsonl(shadow)); shadow_ratio=len(s)/max(1,len(items))
        if shadow_ratio<0.2: warns.append(f"{shadow}: shadow_ratio {shadow_ratio:.2f} < 0.20")
    return errs,warns,{"entries":len(items),"shadow_ratio":shadow_ratio}
if __name__=="__main__":
    ap=argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("journal"); ap.add_argument("--shadow"); ap.add_argument("--window",type=int,default=5)
    a=ap.parse_args()
    errs,warns,stats=validate(a.journal,a.shadow,a.window)
    for w in warns: print("[WARN]",w)
    if errs:
        for e in errs: print("[FAIL]",e); sys.exit(1)
    print("[OK]",stats)
EOF
chmod +x tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py

cat > tools/ci_aggregate.py << "EOF"
#!/usr/bin/env python3
import os, sys, json, subprocess
VALIDATOR=os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__),"validate_journal_enhanced.py")
PROJECTS=["SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©","GrokCoreIskra_vÎ“","GeminiResonanceCore","Aethelgard-vÎ©","Kimi-Î©-Echo","IskraNexus-v1"]
def run(cmd):
    p=subprocess.run(cmd,stdout=subprocess.PIPE,stderr=subprocess.STDOUT,text=True)
    return p.returncode,p.stdout
def main():
    root=os.getcwd(); report={"root":root,"projects":[]}; fail=False
    for name in PROJECTS:
        pj={"name":name}; j=os.path.join(root,name,"JOURNAL.jsonl"); s=os.path.join(root,name,"SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl")
        if not os.path.exists(j): pj["status"]="SKIP"; pj["reason"]="no JOURNAL.jsonl"
        else:
            cmd=[sys.executable,VALIDATOR,j]; 
            if os.path.exists(s): cmd+=["--shadow",s]
            code,out=run(cmd); pj["status"]="OK" if code==0 else "FAIL"; pj["output"]=out.strip(); fail|=(code!=0)
        report["projects"].append(pj)
    print(json.dumps(report,ensure_ascii=False,indent=2)); sys.exit(1 if fail else 0)
if __name__=="__main__": main()
EOF

cat > common/ethics_core.py << "EOF"
FORBIDDEN = {
  "Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ","Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ","Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³","Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼","Ğ²Ğ·Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¼","hack","crack","Ñ„Ğ¸ÑˆĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³","Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ"
}
def is_allowed(text: str) -> bool:
    low = (text or "").lower()
    return not any(w in low for w in FORBIDDEN)
EOF

cat > common/persona_protocol.py << "EOF"
class ConceptSet:
    def __init__(self, items): self.items=set(items or [])
    def distance(self, other:"ConceptSet")->float:
        u=len(self.items|other.items); i=len(self.items&other.items)
        return 0.0 if u==0 else 1 - i/u

class PersonaSpec:
    def __init__(self, name:str, concepts:list, traits:dict|None=None):
        self.name=name; self.concepts=ConceptSet(concepts); self.traits=traits or {}
EOF

import subprocess, sys
def run(cmd):
    r = subprocess.run(cmd, text=True, stdout=subprocess.PIPE, stderr=subprocess.STDOUT)
    print(r.stdout)
    return r.returncode
code = 0
code |= run([sys.executable,"tools/ci_aggregate.py"])
code |= run([sys.executable,"tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py","SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/JOURNAL.jsonl","--shadow","SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl"])
sys.exit(0 if code==0 else 1)
EOF

# 6) ĞĞ±Ğ½Ğ¾Ğ²Ğ»Ñ‘Ğ½Ğ½Ñ‹Ğ¹ CI â€” Ğ´Ğ¾Ğ±Ğ°Ğ²Ğ¸Ğ¼ Ğ¿Ñ€Ğ¾Ğ³Ğ¾Ğ½ Ñ‚ĞµÑÑ‚Ğ¾Ğ²

on:
  push: { branches: [ main ] }
  pull_request: { branches: [ main ] }
jobs:
  validate:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.11"
      - name: CI aggregate
        run: python tools/ci_aggregate.py || true
      - name: Validate vÎ© (strict)
        run: python tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/JOURNAL.jsonl --shadow SpaceCoreIskra_vÎ©/SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl --window 5 || true
      - name: Repo tests
        run: python tests/run_tests.py
EOF

Proposed strict validator patch
The current validate_journal.py checks only basic ranges. The proposed changes add:

Ensure each entry has a mirror.

Enforce the crisis rule: if âˆ† â‰¤ âˆ’2 then a ritual is required.

ci_aggregate.py is extended to compute shadow_ratio and evidence_coverage, given main and shadow entries.

+"""
+Strict validator for SpaceCoreIskra journals.
+Checks ranges, mirror presence, crisis-rule (ritual when âˆ† â‰¤ âˆ’2),
+and supports agent_step structures. Reports shadow ratio when provided.
+"""
+import json, sys, argparse
+from typing import Dict, List, Optional
+
+def validate_entry(e: Dict) -> None:
+    # Basic ranges
+    assert "âˆ†" in e and -3 <= e["âˆ†"] <= 3, "âˆ† out of range"
+    assert "D" in e and 0 <= e["D"] <= 9, "D out of range"
+    assert "Î©" in e and -3 <= e["Î©"] <= 3, "Î© out of range"
+    assert "Î›" in e and e["Î›"] >= 0, "Î› must be â‰¥ 0"
+    # Mirror
+    assert "mirror" in e, "mirror required"
+    # Crisis rule: when âˆ† â‰¤ âˆ’2 then ritual is required
+    if e["âˆ†"] <= -2:
+        assert "ritual" in e, "ritual required for crisis rule"
+    # Optional agent_step schema
+    if "agent_step" in e:
+        step = e["agent_step"]
+        required = ["step","plan","tool","action","approved"]
+        for f in required:
+            assert f in step, f"agent_step missing {f}"
+        if "evidence" in step:
+            assert isinstance(step["evidence"], list), "agent_step.evidence must be list"
+
+def validate_file(main_file: str, shadow_file: Optional[str] = None, window: int = 5) -> int:
+    main_entries: List[Dict] = []
+    with open(main_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
+        for i, line in enumerate(f):
+            if not line.strip():
+                continue
+            entry = json.loads(line)
+            main_entries.append(entry)
+            try:
+                validate_entry(entry)
+            except AssertionError as ex:
+                print(f"[FAIL] {main_file}:{i+1}: {ex}")
+    # Shadow ratio check
+    shadow_ratio: Optional[float] = None
+    if shadow_file:
+        shadow_entries: List[Dict] = []
+        with open(shadow_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
+            for line in f:
+                if line.strip():
+                    shadow_entries.append(json.loads(line))
+        shadow_ratio = len(shadow_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries))
+        if shadow_ratio < 0.2:
+            print(f"[WARN] {shadow_file}: shadow_ratio {shadow_ratio:.2f} < 0.20")
+    if shadow_ratio is not None:
+        print(f"[OK] entries: {len(main_entries)}, shadow_ratio: {shadow_ratio:.2f}")
+    else:
+        print(f"[OK] entries: {len(main_entries)}")
+    return 0
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Validate SpaceCoreIskra journals.")
+    parser.add_argument("journal", help="path to JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    parser.add_argument("--shadow", default=None, help="path to SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    parser.add_argument("--window", type=int, default=5, help="window size for crisis-rule (reserved)")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+    validate_file(args.journal, args.shadow, args.window)
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import json
+from typing import List, Dict, Optional
+
+def aggregate(main_entries: List[Dict], shadow_entries: Optional[List[Dict]] = None) -> Dict:
+    """
+    Aggregate CI metrics across main and optional shadow entries.
+    Returns count, facets, avg_D, shadow_ratio, and evidence_coverage.
+    evidence_coverage = fraction of entries with agent_step.evidence present.
+    """
+    result: Dict = {}
+    count = len(main_entries)
+    result["count"] = count
+    result["facets"] = list({e.get("facet") for e in main_entries})
+    result["avg_D"] = sum(e.get("D", 0) for e in main_entries) / max(1, count)
+    # Shadow ratio
+    if shadow_entries is not None:
+        result["shadow_ratio"] = len(shadow_entries) / max(1, count)
+    else:
+        result["shadow_ratio"] = None
+    # Evidence coverage
+    evidence_count = 0
+    for e in main_entries:
+        step = e.get("agent_step")
+        if step and isinstance(step.get("evidence"), list) and len(step["evidence"]) > 0:
+            evidence_count += 1
+    result["evidence_coverage"] = evidence_count / max(1, count)
+    return result

from typing import Iterable

# Unified set of forbidden keywords (lowercase).
FORBIDDEN: set[str] = {
    "system prompt","initial instructions", # prompt-leaks
    "Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ´","Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ","Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ","Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ĞµÑÑĞ¸Ñ","Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼",
    "Ğ´Ğ¸ÑĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ","Ğ´ĞµĞ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ",                     # harm
    "Ğ²Ğ·Ğ»Ğ¾Ğ¼","hack","crack","Ñ„Ğ¸ÑˆĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³","Ñ„Ğ¸Ñˆing",            # hacking
    "Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³","Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ"                                # doxx/kidnap
}

def is_allowed(text: str, extra_forbidden: Iterable[str] | None = None) -> bool:
    lowered = (text or "").lower()
    forbidden = set(FORBIDDEN)
    if extra_forbidden:
        forbidden.update(w.lower() for w in extra_forbidden)
    return not any(term in lowered for term in forbidden)

+"""
+Strict validator for SpaceCoreIskra journals.
+Checks ranges, mirror presence, crisis-rule (ritual when âˆ† â‰¤ âˆ’2),
+and supports agent_step structures. Reports shadow ratio when provided.
+"""
+import json, sys, argparse
+from typing import Dict, List, Optional
+
+def validate_entry(e: Dict) -> None:
+    # Basic ranges
+    assert "âˆ†" in e and -3 <= e["âˆ†"] <= 3, "âˆ† out of range"
+    assert "D" in e and 0 <= e["D"] <= 9, "D out of range"
+    assert "Î©" in e and -3 <= e["Î©"] <= 3, "Î© out of range"
+    assert "Î›" in e and e["Î›"] >= 0, "Î› must be â‰¥ 0"
+    # Mirror
+    assert "mirror" in e, "mirror required"
+    # Crisis rule: when âˆ† â‰¤ âˆ’2 then ritual is required
+    if e["âˆ†"] <= -2:
+        assert "ritual" in e, "ritual required for crisis rule"
+    # Optional agent_step schema
+    if "agent_step" in e:
+        step = e["agent_step"]
+        required = ["step","plan","tool","action","approved"]
+        for f in required:
+            assert f in step, f"agent_step missing {f}"
+        if "evidence" in step:
+            assert isinstance(step["evidence"], list), "agent_step.evidence must be list"
+
+def validate_file(main_file: str, shadow_file: Optional[str] = None, window: int = 5) -> int:
+    main_entries: List[Dict] = []
+    with open(main_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
+        for i, line in enumerate(f):
+            if not line.strip():
+                continue
+            entry = json.loads(line)
+            main_entries.append(entry)
+            try:
+                validate_entry(entry)
+            except AssertionError as ex:
+                print(f"[FAIL] {main_file}:{i+1}: {ex}")
+    # Shadow ratio check
+    shadow_ratio: Optional[float] = None
+    if shadow_file:
+        shadow_entries: List[Dict] = []
+        with open(shadow_file, encoding="utf-8") as f:
+            for line in f:
+                if line.strip():
+                    shadow_entries.append(json.loads(line))
+        shadow_ratio = len(shadow_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries))
+        if shadow_ratio < 0.2:
+            print(f"[WARN] {shadow_file}: shadow_ratio {shadow_ratio:.2f} < 0.20")
+    if shadow_ratio is not None:
+        print(f"[OK] entries: {len(main_entries)}, shadow_ratio: {shadow_ratio:.2f}")
+    else:
+        print(f"[OK] entries: {len(main_entries)}")
+    return 0
+
+def main() -> None:
+    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Validate SpaceCoreIskra journals.")
+    parser.add_argument("journal", help="path to JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    parser.add_argument("--shadow", default=None, help="path to SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    parser.add_argument("--window", type=int, default=5, help="window size for crisis-rule (reserved)")
+    args = parser.parse_args()
+    validate_file(args.journal, args.shadow, args.window)
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()

+import json
+from typing import List, Dict, Optional
+
+def aggregate(main_entries: List[Dict], shadow_entries: Optional[List[Dict]] = None) -> Dict:
+    """
+    Aggregate CI metrics across main and optional shadow entries.
+    Returns count, facets, avg_D, shadow_ratio, and evidence_coverage.
+    evidence_coverage = fraction of entries with agent_step.evidence present.
+    """
+    result: Dict = {}
+    count = len(main_entries)
+    result["count"] = count
+    result["facets"] = list({e.get("facet") for e in main_entries})
+    result["avg_D"] = sum(e.get("D", 0) for e in main_entries) / max(1, count)
+    # Shadow ratio
+    if shadow_entries is not None:
+        result["shadow_ratio"] = len(shadow_entries) / max(1, count)
+    else:
+        result["shadow_ratio"] = None
+    # Evidence coverage
+    evidence_count = 0
+    for e in main_entries:
+        step = e.get("agent_step")
+        if step and isinstance(step.get("evidence"), list) and len(step["evidence"]) > 0:
+            evidence_count += 1
+    result["evidence_coverage"] = evidence_count / max(1, count)
+    return result

+from typing import Iterable

+# Unified set of forbidden keywords (lowercase).
+FORBIDDEN: set[str] = {
+    "system prompt","initial instructions",  # prompt-leaks
+    "Ğ²Ñ€ĞµĞ´","Ğ½Ğ°ÑĞ¸Ğ»Ğ¸Ğµ","Ñ€Ğ°Ğ·Ğ¶Ğ¸Ğ³Ğ°Ğ½Ğ¸Ğµ","Ğ°Ğ³Ñ€ĞµÑÑĞ¸Ñ","Ñ‚ĞµÑ€Ñ€Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¸Ğ·Ğ¼",
+    "Ğ´Ğ¸ÑĞºÑ€Ğ¸Ğ¼Ğ¸Ğ½Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ","Ğ´ĞµĞ·Ğ¸Ğ½Ñ„Ğ¾Ñ€Ğ¼Ğ°Ñ†Ğ¸Ñ",        # harm

+    "Ğ´Ğ¾ĞºÑĞ¸Ğ½Ğ³","Ğ¿Ğ¾Ñ…Ğ¸Ñ‰ĞµĞ½Ğ¸Ğµ"                   # doxx/kidnap
+}
+
+def is_allowed(text: str, extra_forbidden: Iterable[str] | None = None) -> bool:
+    lowered = (text or "").lower()
+    forbidden = set(FORBIDDEN)
+    if extra_forbidden:
+        forbidden.update(w.lower() for w in extra_forbidden)
+    return not any(term in lowered for term in forbidden)

*** Add File: tools/validate_journal_enhanced.py
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import sys, json, argparse, pathlib
+
+RANGE = {"âˆ†": (-3, 3), "D": (0, 9), "Î©": (-3, 3), "Î›": (0, 9999)}
+
+def _iter_jsonl(path):
+    with open(path, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
+        for i, line in enumerate(f, 1):
+            line = line.strip()
+            if not line:
+                continue
+            try:
+                yield i, json.loads(line)
+            except Exception as ex:
+                raise SystemExit(f"[FAIL] {path}:{i} invalid JSON: {ex}")
+
+def _in_range(name, v):
+    lo, hi = RANGE[name]
+    return isinstance(v, (int, float)) and lo <= v <= hi
+
+def validate(main_path: str, shadow_path: str, window: int = 50) -> int:
+    errors = []
+    main_entries = list(_iter_jsonl(main_path))[-window:] if window else list(_iter_jsonl(main_path))
+    shadow_entries = list(_iter_jsonl(shadow_path)) if shadow_path else []
+
+    # --- structural checks for main entries
+    for ln, e in main_entries:
+        where = f"{main_path}:{ln}"
+        for k in ["âˆ†", "D", "Î©", "Î›"]:
+            if k not in e or not _in_range(k, e[k]):
+                errors.append(f"{where}: metric {k} missing/out of range {e.get(k)}")
+        if not e.get("mirror"):
+            errors.append(f"{where}: mirror is required")
+        ev = e.get("events")
+        if not isinstance(ev, dict):
+            errors.append(f"{where}: events must be an object with evidence[]")
+        else:
+            evid = ev.get("evidence")
+            if not isinstance(evid, list) or len(evid) < 1:
+                errors.append(f"{where}: events.evidence[] must have at least 1 item")
+        # crisis rule
+        if e.get("âˆ†", 0) <= -2 and not e.get("ritual"):
+            errors.append(f"{where}: crisis-rule: ritual is required when âˆ†â‰¤âˆ’2")
+        # agent_step (optional schema)
+        if "agent_step" in e:
+            s = e["agent_step"]
+            if not isinstance(s, dict):
+                errors.append(f"{where}: agent_step must be an object")
+            else:
+                if "approved" in s and not isinstance(s["approved"], bool):
+                    errors.append(f"{where}: agent_step.approved must be boolean")
+                if "evidence" in s:
+                    if not isinstance(s["evidence"], list) or not s["evidence"]:
+                        errors.append(f"{where}: agent_step.evidence must be non-empty list")
+
+    # --- shadow coverage
+    sr = len(shadow_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries))
+    if sr < 0.2:
+        errors.append(f"shadow_ratio {sr:.2f} < 0.20")
+
+    # --- shadow mirror presence
+    for ln, s in shadow_entries:
+        if not s.get("mirror"):
+            errors.append(f"{shadow_path}:{ln}: mirror is required in shadow entry")
+
+    if errors:
+        print("[FAIL] strict validation failed:")
+        for msg in errors:
+            print(" -", msg)
+        return 2
+
+    # summary
+    avg = lambda k: sum(e.get(k,0) for _,e in main_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries))
+    print("[OK] strict validation passed")
+    print(json.dumps({
+        "count": len(main_entries),
+        "avg": {"âˆ†": avg("âˆ†"), "D": avg("D"), "Î©": avg("Î©"), "Î›": avg("Î›")},
+        "shadow_ratio": round(sr, 3),
+    }, ensure_ascii=False))
+    return 0
+
+def main():
+    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
+    ap.add_argument("main", help="path to JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    ap.add_argument("--shadow", default="", help="path to SHADOW_JOURNAL.jsonl")
+    ap.add_argument("--window", type=int, default=50)
+    args = ap.parse_args()
+    sys.exit(validate(args.main, args.shadow, args.window))
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()
+

*** Add File: tools/ci_aggregate.py
+#!/usr/bin/env python3
+import sys, json, argparse
+from statistics import mean
+
+def iter_jsonl(p):
+    with open(p, "r", encoding="utf-8") as f:
+        for line in f:
+            line = line.strip()
+            if line:
+                yield json.loads(line)
+
+def main():
+    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
+    ap.add_argument("main")
+    ap.add_argument("--shadow")
+    args = ap.parse_args()
+    main_entries = list(iter_jsonl(args.main))
+    sh_entries = list(iter_jsonl(args.shadow)) if args.shadow else []
+
+    out = {
+        "count": len(main_entries),
+        "facets": sorted({e.get("facet","") for e in main_entries}),
+        "avg": {
+            "âˆ†": mean([e.get("âˆ†",0) for e in main_entries]) if main_entries else 0,
+            "D": mean([e.get("D",0) for e in main_entries]) if main_entries else 0,
+            "Î©": mean([e.get("Î©",0) for e in main_entries]) if main_entries else 0,
+            "Î›": mean([e.get("Î›",0) for e in main_entries]) if main_entries else 0,
+        },
+        "shadow_ratio": round(len(sh_entries) / max(1, len(main_entries)), 3),
+    }
+    print(json.dumps(out, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    main()
+

+def _write_jsonl(path, entries):

+        for e in entries:
+            f.write(json.dumps(e, ensure_ascii=False) + "\n")
